            entry 10 create
                description "prevent-virus-deny" 
                match 
                    src-ip ip-prefix-list "3001-deny"
                exit 
                action
                    drop
                exit
            exit 
            entry 20 create
                description "prevent-virus-tcp" 
                match protocol tcp
                    dst-port port-list "3001-tcp"
                exit 
                action
                    drop
                exit
            exit 
            entry 30 create
                description "prevent-virus-udp" 
                match protocol udp
                    dst-port port-list "3001-udp"
                exit 
                action
                    drop
                exit
            exit 
            entry 40 create
                match protocol icmp
                    fragment true
                exit 
                action
                    drop
                exit
            exit 
        exit

            exit
